// Description: A configurable WIDTH-bit counter with up/down control, enable, synchronous load and carry out.

`timescale 1ns / 1ps

// ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Module: counter
// Description: A generic up/down counter with configurable width, enable,
//              synchronous load, and carry output.
// ----------------------------------------------------------------------------

module counter #(
    parameter WIDTH = 8  // Counter bit width, adjustable via parameter
)(
    // Clock and reset
    input      clk,        // Positive edge clock
    input      rst_n,      // Active-low asynchronous reset

    // Control signals
    input      en,         // Enable counter operation
    input      up,         // Direction control: 1 for up, 0 for down
    input      load,       // Load input data synchronously

    // Data input
    input  [WIDTH-1:0] data_in,  // Input data for load operation

    // Outputs
    output reg [WIDTH-1:0] count_out,  // Current counter value
    output reg            carry_out   // Carry output (overflow/underflow)
);

// ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Internal Signal Declarations
// ----------------------------------------------------------------------------

reg [WIDTH-1:0] count_reg;  // Internal register for storing the current count value

// ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Counter Logic
// ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
always @(posedge clk or negedge rst_n) begin
    if (!rst_n) begin
        // Asynchronous reset: reset counter to 0
        count_reg   <= {WIDTH{1'b0}};
        carry_out   <= 1'b0;
    end else begin
        if (load) begin
            // Load input data into the counter
            count_reg <= data_in;
            carry_out <= 1'b0;  // No carry during load
        end else if (en) begi...

)(

// File: counter.v
// Description: A configurable up/down counter with enable and reset
// Author: V-Agent
// Date: 2025-08-07

module counter #(
    parameter C_WIDTH = 4,      // Counter width
    parameter C_MAX  = 4'd15     // Maximum count value
)(
    input      clk,             // Clock input
    input      rst_n,            // Active-low reset
    input      en,              // Enable input
    input      up,              // Direction control (1: up, 0: down)
    output reg [C_WIDTH-1:0] q,  // Counter output
    output     carry            // Carry output
);

// Internal signals
wire [C_WIDTH-1:0] next_q;

// Counter behavior
always @(posedge clk or negedge rst_n) begin
    if (!rst_n) begin
        q <= {C_WIDTH{1'b0}};
    end else if (en) begin
        q <= next_q;
    end
end

// Next state logic
assign next_q = (up) ? ((q == C_MAX) ? {C_WIDTH{1'b0}} : q + 1) : 
                     ((q == {C_WIDTH{1'b0}}) ? C_M...

21:34:13 - Agent.enhanced_real_code_review_agent - INFO - ğŸ§  å·²æ·»åŠ æ¨¡å—ä»£ç åˆ°å‚æ•°ï¼Œé•¿åº¦: 3818 å­—ç¬¦
21:34:13 - Agent.enhanced_real_code_review_agent - INFO - ğŸ”§ æ‰§è¡Œå·¥å…·è°ƒç”¨: run_simulation (å°è¯• 1/3)
21:34:13 - Agent.enhanced_real_code_review_agent - INFO - ğŸ” è¿è¡Œä»¿çœŸ: logs/experiment_20250807_212842/artifacts/unknown_module.v logs/experiment_20250807_212842/artifacts/testbench_unknown_module.v // File: counter.v
// Description: A configurable WIDTH-bit counter with up/down control, enable, synchronous load and carry out.

`timescale 1ns / 1ps

// ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Module: counter
// Description: A generic up/down counter with configurable width, enable,
//              synchronous load, and carry output.
// ----------------------------------------------------------------------------

module counter #(
    parameter WIDTH = 8  // Counter bit width, adjustable via parameter
)(
    // Clock and reset
    input      clk,        // Positive edge clock
    input      rst_n,      // Active-low asynchronous reset

    // Control signals
    input      en,         // Enable counter operation
    input      up,         // Direction control: 1 for up, 0 for down
    input      load,       // Load input data synchronously

    // Data input
    input  [WIDTH-1:0] data_in,  // Input data for load operation

    // Outputs
    output reg [WIDTH-1:0] count_out,  // Current counter value
    output reg            carry_out   // Carry output (overflow/underflow)
);

// ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Internal Signal Declarations
// ----------------------------------------------------------------------------

reg [WIDTH-1:0] count_reg;  // Internal register for storing the current count value

// ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Counter Logic
// ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
always @(posedge clk or negedge rst_n) begin
    if (!rst_n) begin
        // Asynchronous reset: reset counter to 0
        count_reg   <= {WIDTH{1'b0}};
        carry_out   <= 1'b0;
    end else begin
        if (load) begin
            // Load input data into the counter
            count_reg <= data_in;
            carry_out <= 1'b0;  // No carry during load
        end else if (en) begin
            // Counting enabled
            if (up) begin
                // Up counting
                if (count_reg == {WIDTH{1'b1}}) begin
                    carry_out <= 1'b1;  // Overflow
                end else begin
                    carry_out <= 1'b0;
                end
                count_reg <= count_reg + 1;
            end else begin
                // Down counting
                if (count_reg == {WIDTH{1'b0}}) begin
                    carry_out <= 1'b1;  // Underflow
                end else begin
                    carry_out <= 1'b0;
                end
                count_reg <= count_reg - 1;
            end
        end else begin
            // Counting disabled, keep current value
            carry_out <= 1'b0;
        end
    end
end

// ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Output Assignments
// ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
assign count_out = count_reg;  // Connect output to internal register

// ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
// End of Module
// ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
endmodule
---

21:34:15 - Agent.enhanced_real_code_review_agent - INFO - ğŸ” è¿è¡Œä»¿çœŸ: logs/experiment_20250807_212842/artifacts/unknown_module.v logs/experiment_20250807_212842/artifacts/testbench_unknown_module.v // File: counter.v
// Description: A configurable WIDTH-bit counter with up/down control, enable, synchronous load and carry out.

`timescale 1ns / 1ps

// ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Module: counter
// Description: A generic up/down counter with configurable width, enable,
//              synchronous load, and carry output.
// ----------------------------------------------------------------------------

module counter #(
    parameter WIDTH = 8  // Counter bit width, adjustable via parameter
)(
    // Clock and reset
    input      clk,        // Positive edge clock
    input      rst_n,      // Active-low asynchronous reset

    // Control signals
    input      en,         // Enable counter operation
    input      up,         // Direction control: 1 for up, 0 for down
    input      load,       // Load input data synchronously

    // Data input
    input  [WIDTH-1:0] data_in,  // Input data for load operation

    // Outputs
    output reg [WIDTH-1:0] count_out,  // Current counter value
    output reg            carry_out   // Carry output (overflow/underflow)
);

// ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Internal Signal Declarations
// ----------------------------------------------------------------------------

reg [WIDTH-1:0] count_reg;  // Internal register for storing the current count value

// ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Counter Logic
// ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
always @(posedge clk or negedge rst_n) begin
    if (!rst_n) begin
        // Asynchronous reset: reset counter to 0
        count_reg   <= {WIDTH{1'b0}};
        carry_out   <= 1'b0;
    end else begin
        if (load) begin
            // Load input data into the counter
            count_reg <= data_in;
            carry_out <= 1'b0;  // No carry during load
        end else if (en) begin
            // Counting enabled
            if (up) begin
                // Up counting
                if (count_reg == {WIDTH{1'b1}}) begin
                    carry_out <= 1'b1;  // Overflow
                end else begin
                    carry_out <= 1'b0;
                end
                count_reg <= count_reg + 1;
            end else begin
                // Down counting
                if (count_reg == {WIDTH{1'b0}}) begin
                    carry_out <= 1'b1;  // Underflow
                end else begin
                    carry_out <= 1'b0;
                end
                count_reg <= count_reg - 1;
            end
        end else begin
            // Counting disabled, keep current value
            carry_out <= 1'b0;
        end
    end
end

// ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Output Assignments
// ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
assign count_out = count_reg;  // Connect output to internal register

// ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
// End of Module
// ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
endmodule
---
